<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d6b2998a-c385-4cf0-8327-d1d395f17820'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

</script>

  <span id="freeText5980158408198094699" style="display:none">Unearthly Beauty There's something strange about the new girls in town. Briar Creek, Oregon, has never seen anything like the supernatural grace of Rowan, Kestrel, and Jade, three sisters who move into the dilapidated old house next to Mark and Mary-Lynnette Carter. Mark is obsessed with Jade-- but she and her sisters have a secret. And when Mark and Mary-Lynnette follow them into the woods one night, they are plunged into a nightmare beyond their imagination. Because the sisters are fugitives from the Night World, and their brother Ash is hot on the trail behind them. He's ruthless, gorgeous, and he has orders to bring the girls back at all costs. And when he sees Mary-Lynette, he decides to take her too...</span>

<div id="review_23779576" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/23779576" />
    <a title="Lucy " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/45923-lucy"><img alt="Lucy " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1300985055p2/45923.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/23779576?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucy " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucy " href="/user/show/45923-lucy">Lucy </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of Twilight</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Lucy  by: </span>
      Shani Kaish
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45923-lucy?shelf=teen">teen</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45923-lucy?shelf=childhood-favorites">childhood-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/45923-lucy?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer23779576" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18061121338822381768">I just reread this book, and I remember now why I liked these so much in high school. These books have everything right about them that is wrong with Twilight. For one, it's over three quarters shorter. But that's just for starters.<br/><br/>Briar Creek is just about the quietest town imagineable, so when Mrs. Burdock's nieces, Rowan, Kestrel and Jade Redfern, move in next door, Mary-Lynnette and her brother Mark are obviously intrigued. They have good reason to be. The Redfern sisters aren't just beautif</span>
  <span id="freeText18061121338822381768" style="display:none">I just reread this book, and I remember now why I liked these so much in high school. These books have everything right about them that is wrong with Twilight. For one, it's over three quarters shorter. But that's just for starters.<br /><br />Briar Creek is just about the quietest town imagineable, so when Mrs. Burdock's nieces, Rowan, Kestrel and Jade Redfern, move in next door, Mary-Lynnette and her brother Mark are obviously intrigued. They have good reason to be. The Redfern sisters aren't just beautiful, they're strange. Different. The Redfern sisters also happen to be vampires on the run, being stalked by their older brother, Ash.<br /><br />The reason these books are so much better than Twilight is partially because of the women. Mary-Lynnette has personality. She has character, and not just because the author wasnts us to know that she's interesting. Mary-Lynnette has <i>interests</i>.<br /><br />Much like Edward and Bella, Mary-Lynnette has an instant connection that she doesn't understand with a vampire--Ash--and also like Edward and Bella, Mary-Lynnette and Ash both at first try to keep apart from each other. But unlike Edward and Bella, we know their reasons, and they actually make sense. We see them change their minds about each other, and we understand why. We see them grow together over the course of this short book, and it makes sense.<br /><br />Ash is hot, of course, but Mary-Lynnette sees right through that. She's too prickly for that. <br /><br /><i>She wasn't impressed by good looks unless they were the thin, brown, and interesting kind...Gorgeous guys--guys who looked like big ash-blond cats--didn't have any reason to develop their minds. They were self-absorbed and vain. With IQs barely high enough to keep a seat warm.</i><br /><br />Mary-Lynnette never falls for Ash because he's a hottie. She is eventually won over by him because of his character, because of parts of who he is--who he <i>really</i> is--that show themselves to her.<br /><br />And, not to mention, this short little book has a lovely bit of female friendship, between Mary-Lynnette and Rowan. Not to mention the sisterly bond between the three different, but strong and interesting each in their own way sisters.<br /><br />This book isn't deep by any stretch of the imagination, but it is a fun fast read. It's what Twilight wishes it could be. I suppose a hundred thousand teenage girls can't be wrong, but I wish I could put the books in this series in their hands instead. They're just so much better on every level.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18061121338822381768" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_3222858665" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3222858665" />
    <a title="Abigail" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/87835420-abigail"><img alt="Abigail" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539121384p2/87835420.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3222858665?book_show_action=true">Mar 08, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Abigail" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Abigail" href="/user/show/87835420-abigail">Abigail</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Teenagers Who Enjoy Vampire/Supernatural Fiction</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87835420-abigail?shelf=werewolves">werewolves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87835420-abigail?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87835420-abigail?shelf=childrens-fiction">childrens-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87835420-abigail?shelf=childrens-fantasy">childrens-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87835420-abigail?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87835420-abigail?shelf=young-adult-romance">young-adult-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3222858665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5391960999336999162">This is the second installment of L.J. Smith's <i>Night World</i> series, which debuted in the mid 1990s, and featured a hidden world of vampires, witches and shape-shifters. When Rowan, Kestrel and Jade Redfern - three beautiful but unearthly sisters - come to live in Briar Creek, Oregon, Mary-Lynette Carter and her brother Mark find themselves drawn into their dangerous secret. Vampires on the run from the restrictive Night World, the three girls and their new friends must confront a possible vampire</span>
  <span id="freeText5391960999336999162" style="display:none">This is the second installment of L.J. Smith's <i>Night World</i> series, which debuted in the mid 1990s, and featured a hidden world of vampires, witches and shape-shifters. When Rowan, Kestrel and Jade Redfern - three beautiful but unearthly sisters - come to live in Briar Creek, Oregon, Mary-Lynette Carter and her brother Mark find themselves drawn into their dangerous secret. Vampires on the run from the restrictive Night World, the three girls and their new friends must confront a possible vampire-hunter, as well as the sinister Ash Redfern, come to recapture the runaways...<br /><br />Smith continues her world-building in <u>Daughters of Darkness</u>, revealing more about the "Night World," with its male chauvinism, and "species bigotry." She builds upon the "Soulmate Principle," which also appeared in <u>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/395873.Secret_Vampire__Night_World___1_" title="Secret Vampire (Night World, #1) by L.J. Smith" rel="nofollow noopener">Secret Vampire</a>
</u>, and in a trend that would continue throughout the series, featured the previous installment's "villain" as the romantic lead. <br /><br />The teen melodrama is a little thick at times, but Smith's narrative has much to recommend it, and I find that I prefer it to the more current (and much more well-known) <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/41865.Twilight__Twilight___1_" title="Twilight (Twilight, #1) by Stephenie Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Twilight</a>
</i> saga. At heart, <i>Night World</i> is about the redemptive power of forbidden love, and features fairly complex characters, some of whom start out bad, but end up good. The girls are usually smart and strong-willed, and the romantic resolutions are not always smooth.<br /><br /><u>Daughters of Darkness</u> stands out in this respect, and has always been one of my favorites. Mary-Lynette is a strong, caring, and very intelligent young woman, and despite her overwhelming "pre-destined" attraction to Ash, she does not surrender any of her principles. Prejudice, whether between different human groups, or between vampire and werewolf, is an "ugly thing," and she has no hesitation in condemning it, even in her soulmate. A brilliant amateur astronomer, she quotes Shakespeare (<i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/47021.The_Taming_of_the_Shrew" title="The Taming of the Shrew by William Shakespeare" rel="nofollow noopener">The Taming of the Shrew</a>
</i>), and responds to Ash's declaration of love with references to <u>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1885.Pride_and_Prejudice" title="Pride and Prejudice by Jane Austen" rel="nofollow noopener">Pride and Prejudice</a>
</u>.<br /><br />Perhaps most impressive of all, Mary-Lynnete decides to stay exactly who she is: <i>"She was Mary-Lynette, and someday she'd discover a supernova or a comet or a black hole, but she'd do it as a human. And Ash would come back next year. And she would always love the night."</i> In short, L.J. Smith offers everything that is missing in Stephanie Meyer's work, and I highly recommend this series to any reader who was dissatisfied with the latter.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5391960999336999162" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3465234186" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

<span id="freeTextContainer5606350916138770569">Well another quick read. As an adult it's not great to me but when i was younger I would have loved it. I liked the start of the story but feel the daughters got lost a bit at the end. I like how all the books are basically a different part of the night world so your not getting bored with the same characters. </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer107204686" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17524768528249731588">As an adult reader I gave this a 2 star because some things were not very logical. The story was well written and as a teen I think I would have given it a 4 maybe even a 5. I would not mind letting my children read this book as the love relationships are based on emotions rather than physical appearance. The relationship between the characters are healthy, for example they do not have the male stalking the female or the female saying she is going to die without the male. Yes that is a compariso</span>
  <span id="freeText17524768528249731588" style="display:none">As an adult reader I gave this a 2 star because some things were not very logical. The story was well written and as a teen I think I would have given it a 4 maybe even a 5. I would not mind letting my children read this book as the love relationships are based on emotions rather than physical appearance. The relationship between the characters are healthy, for example they do not have the male stalking the female or the female saying she is going to die without the male. Yes that is a comparison to the Twilight series, but this series was written long before Twilight was thought of.<br /><br />The parts I did not find logical is the fact the vampire girls were not going to use any of the powers in the new town they moved too. Why not? I get that they did not want to kill their food (people) but why not talk to each other telepathically. What is the point of not doing that? No one would have known they were doing that. Vampires are stronger than people and one girl had a hard time doing a task a human could do without a problem. Another thing that bothered me about this book is Poppy and James are not in this book. There was a thought of them for a second but I would have liked something to let me know how they were doing. Is Poppy still an illegal vampire? Did her dad except them and her living dead situation? I mean so many unanswered questions. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17524768528249731588" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText3071426409131615847" style="display:none">After reading the first book in the Night World series I didn't really know what to expect from the second one, but I was happy when it turned out to be about vampires as well.<br /><br />Reading this book, I was surprised to see a character from the first book in it now acting as a main character. This is something that I find to be very creative of the author. Especially taking into consideration what an impact the events in this book have on that character's attitude and life. A character who is troublesome for someone in the first book suddenly gets placed in the same shoes as that person, a 'taste of their own medicine' so to speak, it's very fitting.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2441847026684387205">This was probably my favorite of the Night World series. I just really liked that Ash HATED humans, but then much to his horror, he found his soul mate in... A HUMAN, and I just loved how he couldn't fight that no matter how much he may have wanted to. And for a refreshing change, I liked that they didn't just "walk away into the sunset" at the end. These aren't the most spectacular, "blow you away" stories, and it's been a few years since I've read this one. I just know the way it made me feel </span>
  <span id="freeText2441847026684387205" style="display:none">This was probably my favorite of the Night World series. I just really liked that Ash HATED humans, but then much to his horror, he found his soul mate in... A HUMAN, and I just loved how he couldn't fight that no matter how much he may have wanted to. And for a refreshing change, I liked that they didn't just "walk away into the sunset" at the end. These aren't the most spectacular, "blow you away" stories, and it's been a few years since I've read this one. I just know the way it made me feel when reading it, and I've never found other books to compare with it! They have a unique "soul mate" factor that I've not found in any other book (not the way this is done). </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3488466409" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17934236718313947447">Mary-Lynette and her brother, Mark, are used to feeling somewhat different to those around them. She is obsessed with star-gazing and he is desperately shy. It’s entirely understandable that they will be curious to see the new arrivals to their quiet town.<br/>What we see is nothing like you might imagine. Their quiet elderly neighbour has told them her three nieces will come and visit. Their arrival to town is memorable, and of course Mary-Lynette’s curiosity knows no bounds.<br/>Before we know it the gi</span>
  <span id="freeText17934236718313947447" style="display:none">Mary-Lynette and her brother, Mark, are used to feeling somewhat different to those around them. She is obsessed with star-gazing and he is desperately shy. It’s entirely understandable that they will be curious to see the new arrivals to their quiet town.<br />What we see is nothing like you might imagine. Their quiet elderly neighbour has told them her three nieces will come and visit. Their arrival to town is memorable, and of course Mary-Lynette’s curiosity knows no bounds.<br />Before we know it the girls have settled into their new home, having made the shocking discovery of their aunt’s body. Unfortunately, it seems someone is hunting them so they have to come up with a plan.<br />As with Secret Vampire everything happens very very quickly. The conflict between the human world and that of the Night World is, again, in evidence. What was interesting in this one was the attempt to develop the character of Ash a little more than we’d had previously.</span>

  <span id="freeText12529525111372147102" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars:</b><br />The mystery element of the book is pretty interesting. The three sisters are intriguing, and Ash, who was introduced in the first book, does a turnabout and becomes a guy any girl would want to marry.<br /><br />Among some of my favorites. The writing is captivating enough to keep you interested until the end and leave you wanting more. It has a fairly original or uniquely well-developed plot. The pretense and romance were well balanced and done with properly distributed amounts of hints, behaviors, and chemistry. sisters(not including Ash),nineteen,tall,slim,stately,gentle,has cinnamon-brown eyes and warm brown hair that cascaded down her back in waves,blossomy skin,does a blood-tie ceremony with Mark and Mary(which will make them families forever with the three sisters)..so they wont betray the 3 vamp sisters,broke NightWorld law by telling Mark and Mary,went to find jeremy and find out more about him.<br /><br />Kestrel: vampire..but part witch,Ash's sister,middle child out of the three sisters(not including Ash),seventeen and has hair the color of old gold sweeping back from her face,eyes when they followed her into the woods and found them feeding on a deer,does a blood-tie ceremony with Mark and Mary(which will make them families forever with the three sisters)..so they wont betray sisters,eighteen,made-vampire,extremely powerful telepath,had a heart like a glacier and he despised humans.<br /><br />Mrs. Burdock/Aunt Opal: vampire,lives in an old Victorian farmhouse,great-aunt of Rowan..Kestrel..Jade.. and Ash,letting her nieces live with her,forgot to pick up her three nieces(causing them to get a ride with 2 strangers..Todd and Vic), skin was like leather: yellow-brown..hard..smooth..and almost shinny,bald,was found by Jade in the cellar dead with a stake through her chest,got buried in the backyard with Jade's two dead kittens.<br /><br />Unde Hodge: told a human about the NightWorld and got staked while alive.<br /><br />Mary-Lynnette Carter: human,Mark's sister,dark black shinny hair,tan,a year and a half older than Mark,interested in astronomy,when saw a jupiter(thought it was a star)..wished for romance for both her and Mark,seventeen-year-old,spyed on the three vampires burying mrs.burdock,gets suspicious and makes Mark go with her over to Mrs.Burdock's house to check out whats going on,senior,goes to Dewitt High School,kicked Ash in the shin when he touched her and she felt a electricity buzz,trys to find Todd and Vic(she thinks they're part of the events the vampire girls were in),went to the garden to dig up the hole to find the body(but she was interupted by a noise and ran into the farmhouse..only to find her brother),follows the three vamp sisters when she and mark saw them carrying a black bag into the woods,saw the three vamps girl feed on a dear in the woods(found out they were vampires),became a tinnie bit vamp(b/c of the blood-tie ceremony) for a few days(since it wears off..but if she gets bitten again in the meanwhile by a vamp she'll turn into one forever),likes Ash(but doesnt know it),barely found out what the black-symbols means and remembers Jeremy wearing one,went to find jeremy and find out more about him,goes stargazing with Ash,Ash's soul-mate(but they went walking instead),kissed Ash for the first time during that walk,wanted Ash to turn her into a vampire(but she wasnt ready so he didnt),got tied up by jeremy while ash was unconcious,dreamed of white sharp teeth a few days back(and found out it was Jeremy she was dreaming about),saved Ash from jeremy by getting silver from her car(the knife) and killing Jeremy.<br /><br />Mark: human,Mary-Lynnette's brother,clear blue snapping eyes,dark black shinny hair,tan,junior,interested in astronomy,when saw a jupiter(thought it was a star)..wished for excitment in his small town,shy,not shy in front of Jade(likes her),goes to Dewitt High School,follows the three vamp sisters into the woods with mary,saw the three vamps girl feed on a dear in the woods(found out they were vampires),became a tinnie bit vamp(b/c of the blood-tie ceremony) for a few days(since it wears off..but if she gets bitten again in the meanwhile by a vamp she'll turn into one forever),went to find jeremy and find out more about him,doesnt become a vampire but is still dating Jade.<br /><br />Ben: Mark's friend.<br /><br />Mr.Carter: Mary and Ben's dad,married.<br /><br />Claudine: Mark's and Mary's stepmother,Belgian and very pretty..with curly dark hair and sparkling-dark eyes,ten years older than MaryLynnette.<br /><br />Vic Kimble: seemed to be about Rowan's age,deeply tan,blond hair and dirty,was with Todd when seeing the three vampire sisters needing a ride..and offered them one,wanted to rape the three sisters(which resulted with him being fed on but not dying..just getting brainwashed).<br /><br />Todd Akers: seemed to be about Rowan's age,deeply tan,brown hair,was with Vic when seeing the three vampire sisters needing a ride..and offered them one,wanted to rape the three sisters(which resulted with him being fed on but not dying..just getting brainwashed).<br /><br />Sheriff Akers: Todd's father,cop.<br /><br />Bunny Marten: pretty, with soft short blond hair,round..dimpled face,blue eyes,works at Briar Creek general store,senior,was hitting on Ash when he was with Mary..Mark..and the 3 sisters trying to find jeremy,uses the same kind of wood that the goat was killed with(so shes one of Mary's suspects).<br /><br />Jeremy Lovett: Mary's crush,human,brown hair,tall,brown eyes with heavy lashes,a loner(he doesnt go out with girls),parents had died in Medford when he was just a baby,nice,works at the gas station,lives alone(parents died and his uncle dissapeared) in the woods,always wears a black ring(it has one of the NightWorld symbols on it..a black Foxglove),a werewolf,likes Mary,knocked Ash unconcious and tied Mary up after their walk(so he can kill Ash and so Mary wont get in the way..reason: he wanted the area all too himself..as in deer,etc),was the one who killed Aunt Opal(he lost his temper when she said her three vamp nieces were coming into his territory),died.<br /><br />Ethyl: one of Aunt Opal's goats,pure white,with a sweet face and a broad forehead,got staked by a person(the same one that staked Opal),had a black-eye symbol in her mouth.<br /><br />Crane Linden: vampire,very kind,has mental problems(he cant read),usually sends mail from the island to aunt opal,helped the 3 vamp girls run away off the island.<br /><br />James Rasmussen: born-vampire(lamia),Poppy's soulmate.<br /><br />Poppy: made-vampire,jame's soulmate.<br /><br />Facts:<br />-After the blood-tie ceremony,if your a human,you turn a tiny bit vamp..but it wears off in a few days.BUT if u get bitten in the meantime..you stay vamp forever.<br />-Danger to different kinds of species: Silver for werewolves,iron for witches ... And wood for vampires.<br />-Soulmates can read each other's minds without even trying.You cant pick your soul-mate..it can be someone u hate.<br />-Symbol of flowers: Witches use black dahlias,werewolves use black foxglove,made vampires use black roses.<br />-There's a chain of dubs called the Black Iris.</span>

<div id="review_1479741975" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1479741975" />
    <a title="Annelise Lestrange" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7842697-annelise-lestrange"><img alt="Annelise Lestrange" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454634045p2/7842697.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1479741975?book_show_action=true">Dec 25, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annelise Lestrange" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annelise Lestrange" href="/user/show/7842697-annelise-lestrange">Annelise Lestrange</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7842697-annelise-lestrange?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7842697-annelise-lestrange?shelf=beautiful-covers">beautiful-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7842697-annelise-lestrange?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7842697-annelise-lestrange?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7842697-annelise-lestrange?shelf=werewolfs">werewolfs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7842697-annelise-lestrange?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7842697-annelise-lestrange?shelf=witches">witches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7842697-annelise-lestrange?shelf=monsters">monsters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7842697-annelise-lestrange?shelf=royalty">royalty</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1479741975" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4628085747608015514">Review originally posted on <a href='http://www.anneliselestrange.wordpress.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Book Adventures of Annelise Lestrange</a> :)<br/><br/><br/><b>The Story</b><br/><br/>Rowan, Kestrel, and Jade know that they are taking a path of no return when they flee their home. The three sisters are well aware of all the risks and sacrifices involved, but anything in the human world is better than to live in an eternal bubble without any real living.<br/><br/>What they didn’t expect was to have a nosy neighbor.<br/><br/>Mary-Lynnette is a loner, a creature of the night. The stars are her best friends, along with </span>
  <span id="freeText4628085747608015514" style="display:none">Review originally posted on <a href="http://www.anneliselestrange.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">The Book Adventures of Annelise Lestrange</a> :)<br /><br /><br /><b>The Story</b><br /><br />Rowan, Kestrel, and Jade know that they are taking a path of no return when they flee their home. The three sisters are well aware of all the risks and sacrifices involved, but anything in the human world is better than to live in an eternal bubble without any real living.<br /><br />What they didn’t expect was to have a nosy neighbor.<br /><br />Mary-Lynnette is a loner, a creature of the night. The stars are her best friends, along with her brother Mark. Or so she thought, until meeting her three new and inhumanly beautiful neighbors. The girls seem to be nice enough despite all oddities surrounding their family, but can Mary-Lynnette handle with their older brother…?<br /><br />Ash knew he was doomed in the moment he laid eyes on Mary-Lynnette. Once, he had heard from a cousin how he would fall hard for his soul mate, but never believed in such crap. He was a man in a mission and Mary-Lynnette couldn’t be related to his difficulties in taking his sisters back home.<br /><br />Or could she?<br /><br /><br /><b>The Analysis</b><br /><br /><i>Just remembering that those were my impressions and opinion as a reader :)</i><br /><br />OMG, WHY DID I TAKE SO DAMN LONG TO READ THIS SERIES?! IT’S EVEN BETTER THAN THE VAMPIRE DIARIES! (Just don’t tell this to television guys, they will screw this up, haha!). I loved everything aspect of this book and can’t wait to finish Spellbinder, the next book :) Ash was perfection since Secret Vampire, but in this one is where I fell hard for him… *sighs in pure love* I’ll try to do a good job here, but it is so damn difficult when all I feel like doing is fangirling non-stop about Ash, haha!<br /><br />The narrative was my favorite one: third person with alternating points of view. I wish there were more parts under Ash’s POV, but I understand that not knowing much about him it’s part of his charm. Putting more parts under his view would have bared him too much for the reader and all, haha! But one can dream, right? ;)<br /><br />The plot wasn’t overly complicated and quite predictable, but there is a little twist in the end that caught me off guard and this was awesome &lt;3 I don’t really mind simple plots as long as they are well executed and hold my attention while I read. I can even know how it all will end, but I always get curious to see how the outcome shall arrive, haha! My point? There is no lost trip for me, haha!<br /><br />The characters are the high point in this book. Rowan, Kestrel and Jade are unique and each represent a type of person: Rowan is gentle and naïve despite being the oldest; Kestrel is ruthless and savage; and Jade is dreamy and brave. They complement each other in such a perfect way! Mark was also a pleasant enough character and I really liked Jeremy despite everything. And, of course, there is their older brother Ash, but never fear, I’ll get to him. I really liked Mary-Lynnette. She was such a strong heroine for a Young Adult book but without losing her teenager spirit. I could have never made her final decision on the end of the book and I will admire her for this till the world ends.<br /><br />Now, let’s go to Ash. Oh, Ash. He is the lost cousin of Damon Salvatore, I assure you. The difference between them is that Damon is actually a pretty nice guy trying to fool people into believing that he is a demon and Ash is actually a demon trying to fool people into believing that he is a pretty nice guy, haha! ;) Mary-Lynnette described him as a royal cat with ever-changing eye colors and this is the most accurate description ever. Ash has his own pace for everything (cof except when it comes to Mary-Lynnette cof) and never has a permanent eye color – not even in his full vampire form. The strange thing about him is that he is both intelligent and not stubborn at all. He sees something that he is doing wrong and he promptly fixes it instead of insisting that he is right. Not many males have this blessed ability, haha!<br /><br />I really think that L. J. Smith rocked in the Night World series so far and dare to say that those books are a must-read if you love Y&amp;A, romance, Vampires, Witches, Werewolves and really cool humans, haha!<br /><br />That’s it! Thanks for reading &lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="4628085747608015514" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1412200235" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5151279371874737173"><a href='http://psilovethatbook.blogspot.co.uk' rel='nofollow noopener'>MORE? MORE! @ P.S. I love that book!</a><br/><br/> EXPECTATIONS: First of all these covers are so terrible, just look at it. If I saw this in the shop there is no way I would buy it. Fortunately I have three bind ups of this series and each contains three books so I don't have to suffer looking at original covers, the bind ups are black and kinda decent looking. <br/><br/>THE WORLD: Alright so as the series title indicates it is all about the Night World. Which really is just a world of paranormal existing next to our </span>
  <span id="freeText5151279371874737173" style="display:none"><a href="http://psilovethatbook.blogspot.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">MORE? MORE! @ P.S. I love that book!</a><br /><br /> EXPECTATIONS: First of all these covers are so terrible, just look at it. If I saw this in the shop there is no way I would buy it. Fortunately I have three bind ups of this series and each contains three books so I don't have to suffer looking at original covers, the bind ups are black and kinda decent looking. <br /><br />THE WORLD: Alright so as the series title indicates it is all about the Night World. Which really is just a world of paranormal existing next to our usual world. Basically we have vampires, werewolves, witches and what not. Now this is not really different to the usual style we are used to except for the witches, usually when it comes to paranormal books that have vampires and werewolves it is pretty rare to see also witches in them. Anyways, presence of witches of course makes me extremely happy. Anyways, as in the the first book of this series we are still following vampires which in my opinion is pretty cool, who does not love themselves some old style fangs? :D<br /><br />CHARACTERS: I am not sure how many main characters are in this book. We have three sisters Rowan, Kestrel and Jade and then there is their brother Ash and additionally we also have Mark and Mary. To be honest they all play kinda equal role so I am not sure...let's briefly talk about all of them I guess. So the three sisters are pretty similar, they are running from the Night World and discover their aunt dead when they arrive in the small town. Mark and Mary are the neighbors of the aunt and so they meet the new sisters too and discover their secret. Ash on the other hand is coming to get his sisters back to the Night World so they don't get punished. Pretty simple actually except we again get the soulmate nonsense and yeah...let's just say soulmates is apparently the main these of this series and I am not a fan, not at all actually. But all in all, I had no problem with the characters, they did not stand out for me but they were also not annoying. Usual L.J. Smith style I must admit. <br /><br />ROMANCE: Soulmates or insta love or love from the first site or one true love...#puke. One thing that L.J. Smith books and The Vampire Diaries TV show apparently has is this soulmates nonsense. I cannot stand it. The romance suddenly becomes the dumbance. <br /><br />GOOD: I found this story to be rather simple but enjoyable. If you are under stress all day and just want something light and paranormal this is just a perfect read for it. <br /><br />BAD: Again soulmates instalove one true none bullshit. I cannot. I finished reading today the 5th book of the series and I am telling you, soulmates is the topic of this series. Makes me want to puke. <br /><br />OVERALL: If you are a fan of L.J. Smith writing style or just relaxing paranormal reads I would really recommend it. There is not much idiocy apart from mentioned soulmates and it does not feel stretched. <br /><br /><a href="http://psilovethatbook.blogspot.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">MORE? MORE! @ P.S. I love that book!</a></span>

<div id="review_144780718" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/144780718?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="VampireNovelFan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="VampireNovelFan" href="/user/show/4897902-vampirenovelfan">VampireNovelFan</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4897902-vampirenovelfan?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4897902-vampirenovelfan?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer144780718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17292081380195253763">Book 2 of the Night World series, Daughters of Darkness, shifts focus to a new set of characters of the secret society. Relatives of James from the first book, we meet Rowan, Kestrel, and Jade. They are three vampire sisters who snuck away from home. Tired of the secret society, they want to try to live as humans out in Oregon. They move into a dilapidated old home, next to Mark and Mary-Lynette Carter. As Jade and Mark get closer, their brother Ash comes to town to bring his sisters back. Of co</span>
  <span id="freeText17292081380195253763" style="display:none">Book 2 of the Night World series, Daughters of Darkness, shifts focus to a new set of characters of the secret society. Relatives of James from the first book, we meet Rowan, Kestrel, and Jade. They are three vampire sisters who snuck away from home. Tired of the secret society, they want to try to live as humans out in Oregon. They move into a dilapidated old home, next to Mark and Mary-Lynette Carter. As Jade and Mark get closer, their brother Ash comes to town to bring his sisters back. Of course, he meets Mary-Lynette and things get interesting...<br /><br />Ash, the handsome blondie who we remember from the first book as being a conniving, selfish, and manipulative, experiences a bit of growth in this book. In the first book you would have never thought it would happen, but I was glad to see the character development.<br /><br />What I like about the Night World books is that while you could read each book separately as a stand-alone, it's great to see prior plot lines and character weaved into the current story. It makes you feel even more connected to the story and the world. <br /><br />These books are short reads, but I find them pretty satisfying because the plot moves along and it focuses on what you really want to see. <br /><br />*Review also posted to <a href="http://www.amazon.com/review/RGXZEO25QVEFI/ref=cm_cr_rdp_perm" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a></span>

<div id="review_1756256372" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1756256372" />
    <a title="Nikki" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29166340-nikki"><img alt="Nikki" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1438297005p2/29166340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1756256372?book_show_action=true">Sep 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nikki" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nikki" href="/user/show/29166340-nikki">Nikki</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1756256372" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13508685587354442619">After reading the secret vampire I went straight into this because I really enjoyed smiths writing. <br/><br/>The plot for this thankfully was a little different to the normal paranormal it was much more mysterious and I loved it. Three supernaturals come to a deadbeat town in the country and well bring a whole load of drama to it to. <br/><br/>Jade seemed very innocent, bubbly and naive but I think that was very much part of her charm, especially for Mark.<br/><br/>Kestrel seemed wild and fiery so like an animal it was hard</span>
  <span id="freeText13508685587354442619" style="display:none">After reading the secret vampire I went straight into this because I really enjoyed smiths writing. <br /><br />The plot for this thankfully was a little different to the normal paranormal it was much more mysterious and I loved it. Three supernaturals come to a deadbeat town in the country and well bring a whole load of drama to it to. <br /><br />Jade seemed very innocent, bubbly and naive but I think that was very much part of her charm, especially for Mark.<br /><br />Kestrel seemed wild and fiery so like an animal it was hard to really define her as a person.<br /><br />Mary-Lynette now her I loved, she was intelligent a loner but loved what she spent her time on and even though felt many times shed lost who she was I don't think she really did, she was strong minded and when confused it was believable as most teenage angst is. The reaction she had to Ash actually made me laugh a lot and I love that he was meek and kind of mellow around her I mean he completely dropped his attitude around her, yes he was more powerful than her but she didn't cower and run from him she stood her ground and told him when he was being a jerk. <br /><br />Overall this was a quick read, probably could have done with a few more descriptive scenes and more storyline but as short as it was I wasn't disappointed will be reading more by this author. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13508685587354442619" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer480736604464336567">Imagine living in a small town where nothing happens, and then suddenly becoming involved in something beyond your wildest dreams. Welcome to Mary-Lynnette's life in *Daughters of Darkness*.<br/><br/>In this book, she sees the nieces of her neighbor burying what appears to be a bagged body, and she decides to investigate. But, she gets caught. In true L.J. Smith fashion, this leads to the sisters--who are vampire-witch girls--agreeing to form blood ties with ML and her brother, Mark.<br/><br/>It gets even more comp</span>
  <span id="freeText480736604464336567" style="display:none">Imagine living in a small town where nothing happens, and then suddenly becoming involved in something beyond your wildest dreams. Welcome to Mary-Lynnette's life in *Daughters of Darkness*.<br /><br />In this book, she sees the nieces of her neighbor burying what appears to be a bagged body, and she decides to investigate. But, she gets caught. In true L.J. Smith fashion, this leads to the sisters--who are vampire-witch girls--agreeing to form blood ties with ML and her brother, Mark.<br /><br />It gets even more complicated as the truth comes out. Mark's soulmate in life turns out to be Jade, a beauty among the 3 sisters, and ML's soulmate turns out to be the trio of sisters's brother, Ash.<br /><br />And, they all need to know who killed the sisters's great-aunt. They do eventually do so, but first comes some alone time for ML and Ash, in which he decides she should be turned into a vampire, and begins to do so. But, they're interrupted by her friend Jeremy, who turns out to be a werewolf, that wants to kill Ash, pretty much because he wants ML for himself. But, after her car burning and some fighting, ML defeats Jeremy and saves Ash.<br /><br />Afterwards, all is well. Ash explains it all to the elders, like he defeated the werewolf, and then bids farewell to ML for a year.</span>

    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hOiaU5lyoVWXpnvqAUEf7Tfkmn7gjMi2tgR//KG8QL/5kCOlzGTznB+i+hXDlNfnFhi6uuomvl1TqW0gKWA4uA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('c7Y2i8QtPI4yOl1YyBtVWieSA0O3itS/PdhOull0x+cOzo99kTtuR7o+3KcKzp1QBm4jh70golTYdVxm0ai/4A==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer9347123629925992916">I have a new blog about my Vampire Diaries fanfic.<br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/5539821-l-j-smith-s-new-vampires-diaries-series'>https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog...</a><br/><br/><b>L.J. SMITH</b>, Lisa Jane Smith, is the New York Times #1 Bestselling author of <i>The Vampire Diaries, The Secret Circle, The Forbidden Game, Dark Visions, Wildworld</i> and <i>Night World</i> series. She has written over two dozen books for children and young adults, and has enjoyed writing every one of them. She lives in th</span>
  <span id="freeText9347123629925992916" style="display:none">I have a new blog about my Vampire Diaries fanfic.<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/5539821-l-j-smith-s-new-vampires-diaries-series">https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog...</a><br /><br /><b>L.J. SMITH</b>, Lisa Jane Smith, is the New York Times #1 Bestselling author of <i>The Vampire Diaries, The Secret Circle, The Forbidden Game, Dark Visions, Wildworld</i> and <i>Night World</i> series. She has written over two dozen books for children and young adults, and has enjoyed writing every one of them. She lives in the Bay Area of California, with a backyard that is full of flowers, which she adores, especially with many different shades of roses.<br /><br />She loves to visit a friend's little cabin in the Point Reyes National Seashore area, which has lots of trees, lots of animals, lots of beaches to walk on, and lots of places to hike. Once, while hiking, she saw a snow-white buck which allowed her to follow it nearly half a mile. She also likes to collect things: angels (they remind her of her late mother), tiny boxes from different countries or of fanciful shape, nineteenth century children's literature, and books about quantum physics--especially about the mystery of the dark energy in the universe. A militant optimist, she is also part of the Velociraptor Sisterhood (a fancy way of saying that she likes to read, write and discuss books with strong female characters), and she has traveled extensively in Europe and the Far East. The two countries she loves to visit most are Great Britain, with its historic monuments and amazing country landscapes, and Japan, with its bustling urban life and exquisite mountain scenery.<br /><br />Her favorite current writer is Terry Pratchett, the author of the Discworld series, for its wild and witty satires on life, death, war, love, assassins, coppers, and Australia. Her favorite classical writer is Jane Austen. Her favorite poets are Robert Frost and Emily Dickinson. Her favorite movies are The Seven Samurai and Avatar (analyze that!). She doesn't have a favorite TV show, because she doesn't have time to watch TV (and only owns one for playing movies).<br /><br />Her favorite people are her readers, each of whom she cherishes with deep and lasting affection.<br /><br /><i>Note: L. J. Smith wrote books 1-7 of The Vampire Diaries series. After that, a ghostwriter took over the rest of the series. L. J. wrote books 1-3 of The Secret Circle series. After that, a ghostwriter took over the rest of the series. L. J. did not write any of the Originals or Stefan's Diaries. These were written by Kevin Williamson and/or various ghostwritters.</i> <br /></span>

      $('bookCover_3326897').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });
